Let's talk about the room cleaning service. Normally, check out is at noon. I went out in the morning and came back at about 10 o'clock. I found that the door of the guest room was open and there was no one inside. Fortunately, I took my things away when I left in the morning. I shouted a few times before I saw the waiter coming out of another room. I explained that it was the room cleaning, and I opened the door to get the tools. People who have stayed in a hotel know that the room cleaning is to push a tool cart and park it at the door of the room to be cleaned. The most important thing is that I stayed for one day, and I had not checked out at that time. The waiter must not be unaware. Fortunately, I booked a day in this hotel.
